<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:grammatica.html>grammatica</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skilled in writing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράμμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grámma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">line of writing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gráphō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gerebh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scratch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gramschap.html>gramschap</a></i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ire, anger, wrath
<ul><li>Dorothée Sturkenboom, <i>Spectators <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hartstocht.html>hartstocht</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:sekse.html>sekse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:emotionele.html>emotionele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achttiende.html>achttiende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></i>, 1998, 103.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a> (7372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">garnate</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grenate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grenat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pomus granatus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seeded apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaten.html>granaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A grenade; e.g. a hand grenade, an artillery shell.</li>
<li>A garnet.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">granaatsteen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pomegranate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The pomegranate plant, <i>Punica granatum</i>.

***granaatappel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a> (92814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">garnate-appel</i>, also in phrases like <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:appelen.html>appelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> gernaten</i>. A partial loan-translation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pume grenate</i>, also found as simply <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grenate</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappels.html>granaatappels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">granaatappelen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">granaatappelke</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The fruit pomegranate.</li>
<li>The plant Punica granatum, which produces it.</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">granaatboom</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">granaatappelboom</span></li></ul>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a> (69786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genericization of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granola" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granola"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>Granola</a></a></i>, name of an early <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> of the cereal, itself a variation of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granula" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granula">Granula</a></i>, invented by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Caleb_Jackson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Caleb Jackson">James Caleb Jackson</a> in 1863. <i>Granula</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> named after the <span class="Latn" lang="en">granules</span> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Graham_flour" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Graham flour">Graham flour</a>, the main ingredient<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">granolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A breakfast and snack food consisting of loose, <a href = vnd.unilang:crispy.html>crispy</a> pellets made of <a href = vnd.unilang:nuts.html>nuts</a>, rolled oats, honey and other natural ingredients.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Canada, US<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Eating healthy food, supporting the protection of the environment, and having liberal views.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You see more and more of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hippie.html>hippie</a> activist <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> these days.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> November 21,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jame.html>Jame</a> Schaefer |  Tobias Winright,  <cite>Environmental Justice and Climate Change</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=zG1BAgAAQBAJ">[2]</a></sup>, page 228:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>behind them a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>-looking mom in denim <a href = vnd.unilang:overalls.html>overalls</a> and a t-shirt <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pulling in to do her drop-off . . . from a <a href = vnd.unilang:prius.html>Prius</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b> February 13,  Dennis Saffran,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://thefederalist.com/2015/02/13/the-orwellian-campaign-to-project-anti-vaccination-onto-republicans/">The Orwellian Campaign To Project Anti-Vaccination Onto Republicans</a>”, in  <cite>The Federalist</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Rather, the anti-vax movement <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> almost entirely a phenomenon of the affluent <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> Left—as everyone across the political spectrum acknowledged until the last week or so.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2020</b> June 18,  Kiera <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>Butler</a>,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2020/06/the-anti-vax-movements-radical-shift-from-crunchy-granola-purists-to-far-right-crusaders/">The Anti-Vax Movement’s Radical Shift From <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>Crunchy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>Granola</a> Purists to Far-Right Crusaders</a>”, in  <cite>Mother Jones</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yet some <a href = vnd.unilang:experts.html>experts</a> believe that <a href = vnd.unilang:voices.html>voices</a> from the far right are beginning to drown out those of the <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> crowd.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***grapjas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grapjas.html>grapjas</a> (7371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grap.html>grap</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jas.html>jas</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grapjas.html>grapjas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grapjassen.html>grapjassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grapjas.html>grapjasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:joker.html>joker</a>, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> jokes. <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a> (42223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grape</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">grappas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An Italian grape-based spirit of between 80 and 100 proof, made from the distillation of pomace.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A variety or serving of <a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> February 14,  Florence Fabricant,  “Off the Menu”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/02/14/dining/14off.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Wines, a few <a href = vnd.unilang:cocktails.html>cocktails</a> and <b>grappas</b> but no mixed drinks: 34 Downing Street (Bedford Street)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***grasshopper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> (69784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gressehopper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:grashopper.html>grashopper</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashoppyr</i>, alteration of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashope</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashoppe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">greshoppe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">græshoppa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gærshoppa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grass</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Gäärshupper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">grashupper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">grashipper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Grashüpper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Gresshüpper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grashüpfer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">græshoppe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">gräshoppa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">gresshoppe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">grasshoppers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A herbivorous insect of the order Orthoptera, noted for its ability to jump long <a href = vnd.unilang:distances.html>distances</a> and for the habit of some species communicating by stridulation; they are related to but distinct from <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a>.
<ol><li>In the strict sense, refers to insects in the suborder Caelifera, particularly those in the family Acrididae.</li>
<li>In a <a href = vnd.unilang:looser.html>looser</a> sense, also includes the katydids (also known as longhorned grasshoppers or bush <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a>), which are members of the family Tettigoniidae, of the suborder Ensifera.</li></ol>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grasshop</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">locust</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A cocktail made with crème <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:menthe.html>menthe</a> and optionally with crème <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cacao.html>cacao</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young student in initial <a href = vnd.unilang:stages.html>stages</a> of training who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> chosen on account of their obvious <a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a>.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, B.P. Terpstra, <i>Quadrant</i>, November 2009, No. 461 (Volume LIII, Number 11), Quadrant Magazine Limited, page 2:
<dl><dd>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know exactly <i>why</i> Li <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chosen to dance, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> witness a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> assuring <a href = vnd.unilang:officials.html>officials</a> that the child isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> from bourgeois stock. Phew. There are no known landowners in the family, so the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:passes.html>passes</a> some cultural purity test, in a state often fixated on class warfare, driven by the cult of personality, and bullied by <a href = vnd.unilang:paranoia.html>paranoia</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In ordinary square or upright pianos of London make, the escapement <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a>, so made that it can be <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> out and replaced with the key.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Grove to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">grasshop</span></li></ul>
</body>

***grauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grauw.html>grauw</a> (36067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grau.html>grau</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grāo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grēwaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grauw.html>grauw</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grauw.html>grauwer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">grauwst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(literally) grey, not brightly colored, ashen, grubby, grimy</li>
<li>(figuratively) dreary, grim, gloomy, desperate
<dl><dd><i>In Victoriaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:sloppenwijk.html>sloppenwijken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grauwe.html>grauwe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lompen.html>lompen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekenen.html>tekenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grauwe.html>grauwe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:armoede.html>armoede</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moderne.html>moderne</a> favella <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:felle.html>felle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleuren.html>kleuren</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>In Victorian slums grey <a href = vnd.unilang:rags.html>rags</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a> indicative of grim poverty, in a modern favella one <a href = vnd.unilang:sees.html>sees</a> mostly bright colors</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the colour grey</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> gravel (9598)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grasen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grason</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grasōną</i>, akin to modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">graze</span>.

***greep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a> (3389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gripi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grasp, clutch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gripiz</i>. A variant nominative singular form, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preserved in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grepen.html>grepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>grasp, clutches
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houvast.html>houvast</a></span></span></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you have a good <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></b> on the case?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grēpa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">handle, <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*graipō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grepen.html>grepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a>, handle
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handvat.html>handvat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> singular past indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In the sense of random guess, only the example provided <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common usage. For example, while you can say <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gok.html>gok</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gooi.html>gooi</a></i> (take a guess), you can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> say <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijpende.html>grijpende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omvatten.html>omvatten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bemachtigen.html>bemachtigen</a></li>
<li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanvatten.html>aanvatten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hanteren.html>hanteren</a></li>

***grein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a> (129989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grain</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grānum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵr̥h₂nóm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublette with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graan.html>graan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which descended directly from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grānum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>greinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>greintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a small something; a grain</li></ol>
